info:Hawaii Luxury King Room

info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 26, 2023
msg:The hotel design is modern and simple, natural and not tacky. The location is in the city center, very convenient for transportation and walking. There are various restaurants and shops just outside the hotel, depar**ent stores and other shopping malls are just a few steps away, and People's Park is 2 blocks east. It is very convenient to go anywhere. It is less than 10 minutes from the train station and 25 minutes from the airport.
When I made the reservation, I saw that it was the number one high-end hotel in Mudanjiang. I was very lucky to meet the front desk manager Xiao Chi. She learned that I was traveling to Mudanjiang with my family and children, and she took the initiative to upgrade my room type. The service was warm and big. Very loving, thumbs up for her. The little robot responsible for delivering express takeaways in the store is very cute, and children like it very much. There are a few small things that I hope the hotel management will pay attention to. They are not problems, I just hope they can be improved. 1. The breakfast varieties in the hotel are somewhat single, and there are still gaps between them and first-class international hotels. For example, there is no handmade bread, no cheese, no cereal, etc. 2. The service awareness and attitude of the hotel waiters need to be strengthened. For example, the room attendant did not make any move to block the door when seeing a child entering the elevator that was about to close. Overall, the hotel is very good. I will still choose to stay here next time I come to Mudanjiang.
